!= nil {\n62: \t\tkr.log.Error(\"Error downloading plugin manifest keys\", \"error\", err)\n63: \t}\n64: \n65: \t// calculate initial send delay\n66: \tlastUpdated, err := kr.kv.GetLastUpdated(ctx)\n67: \tif err != nil {\n68: \t\treturn err\n69: \t}\n70: \tnextSendInterval := time.Until(lastUpdated.Add(publicKeySyncInterval))\n71: \tif nextSendInterval < time.Minute {\n72: \t\tnextSendInterval = time.Minute\n73: \t}\n74: \n75: \tdownloadKeysTicker := time.NewTicker(nextSendInterval)\n76: \tdefer downloadKeysTicker.Stop()\n77: \n78: \tselect {\n79: \tcase \t\treturn ctx.Err()\n91: \t}\n92: \n93: \treturn ctx.Err()\n94: }\n95: \n96: func (kr *KeyRetriever) updateKeys(ctx context.Context) error {\n97: \tkr.lock.Lock()\n98: \tdefer kr.lock.Unlock()\n99: \n100: \tlastUpdated, err := kr.kv.GetLastUpdated(ctx)\n101: \tif err != nil {\n102: \t\treturn err\n103: \t}\n104: \tif !kr.cfg.PluginForcePublicKeyDownload && time.Since(lastUpdated) < \t}\n155: \n156: \tcachedKeys, err := kr.kv.ListKeys(ctx)\n157: \tif err != nil {\n158: \t\treturn err\n159: \t}\n160: \n161: \tshouldKeep := make(map[string]bool)\n162: \tfor _, key := range multi-layer system spanning manifest signing, signature validation on load, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n## Plugin Manifest Signing and Validation\\n\\nThe core signature verification logic resides in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`. The `Signature` struct implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface and contains:\\n\\n- `Calculate()`: Orchestrates the signature calculation process by reading the MANIFEST.txt file and verifying its PGP signature\\n- `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`: Loads and parses the MANIFEST.txt file from the plugin filesystem\\n- `readPluginManifest()`: Decodes the PGP-signed manifest using clearsign format\\n- `validateManifest()`: Validates manifest fields (plugin, version, keyId, time, files)\\n- `Verify()`: Performs PGP signature verification using OpenPGP cryptography\\n- `verifyHash()`: Verifies SHA256 hashes of individual plugin files against manifest entries\\n\\nThe `PluginManifest` struct defines manifest structure with support for both V1 (deprecated) and V2 formats, including fields for signature type, signing organization, and root URLs (for private plugins).\\n\\n## Signature Validation on Load\\n\\nPlugin signature validation during load is handled by `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`. The `Validation` struct implements the `Validator` interface with:\\n\\n- `ValidateSignature()`: Main validation method that checks signature status and handles inheritance for nested plugins\\n  - Returns success for valid signatures\\n  - Returns success for core/internal plugins\\n  - Returns success for inherited valid signatures from parent plugins\\n  - Calls `CanLoadPlugin()` for unsigned plugins to check the allowlist\\n  - Returns errors for invalid and modified signatures\\n\\n## Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe allowlist enforcement is implemented in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`. The `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct provides:\\n\\n- `CanLoadPlugin()`: Authorizes plugin loading by:\\n  - Allowing all non-unsigned plugins\\n  - Allowing unsigned plugins in dev mode\\n  - Checking if the plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n  - Denying unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\n- `ProvideOSSAuthorizer()`: Factory function creating the authorizer from `PluginManagementCfg`\\n\\nThe allowlist configuration is loaded in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` from the `[plugins]` section's `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting, which accepts a comma-separated list of plugin IDs. The list is stored in `pkg/plugins/config/config.go` as `PluginsAllowUnsigned` in `PluginManagementCfg`.\\n\\n## Key Management\\n\\nPublic key retrieval for signature verification is handled through a two-tier system:\\n\\n1. **Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Contains a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key used as fallback\\n2. **Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches keys from the Grafana.com API, updating every 10 days\\n\\nThe key retriever service (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`) acts as a facade, selecting between dynamic and static retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nSignature calculation and validation are integrated into the plugin loading pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` calls `SignatureCalculator.Calculate()` to determine the plugin's signature status before creating the plugin object\\n\\n2. **Validation Stage** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`): `SignatureValidationStep()` creates a validation function that calls `Validation.ValidateSignature()` for each plugin\\n\\n3. **Configuration Integration** (`pkg/plugins/config/config.go`): `PluginManagementCfg` passes the allowlist to the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer`\\n\\n## Models and Interfaces\\n\\nKey types are defined in `pkg/plugins/models.go`:\\n- `SignatureStatus`: \\\"internal\\\", \\\"valid\\\", \\\"invalid\\\", \\\"modified\\\", \\\"unsigned\\\"\\n- `SignatureType`: \\\"grafana\\\", \\\"commercial\\\", \\\"community\\\", \\\"private\\\", \\\"private-glob\\\"\\n\\nCore interfaces in `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`:\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes plugin loading\\n- `SignatureCalculator`: Calculates plugin signature state\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Stores cached public keys\\n\\n## API and Settings\\n\\nThe plugin API (`pkg/api/plugins.go`) and frontend settings (`pkg/api/frontendsettings.go`) expose plugin signature information. multi-layer system spanning manifest signing, signature validation on load, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n## Plugin Manifest Signing and Validation\\n\\nThe core signature verification logic resides in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`. The `Signature` struct implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface and contains:\\n\\n- `Calculate()`: Orchestrates the signature calculation process by reading the MANIFEST.txt file and verifying its PGP signature\\n- `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`: Loads and parses the MANIFEST.txt file from the plugin filesystem\\n- `readPluginManifest()`: Decodes the PGP-signed manifest using clearsign format\\n- `validateManifest()`: Validates manifest fields (plugin, version, keyId, time, files)\\n- `Verify()`: Performs PGP signature verification using OpenPGP cryptography\\n- `verifyHash()`: Verifies SHA256 hashes of individual plugin files against manifest entries\\n\\nThe `PluginManifest` struct defines manifest structure with support for both V1 (deprecated) and V2 formats, including fields for signature type, signing organization, and root URLs (for private plugins).\\n\\n## Signature Validation on Load\\n\\nPlugin signature validation during load is handled by `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`. The `Validation` struct implements the `Validator` interface with:\\n\\n- `ValidateSignature()`: Main validation method that checks signature status and handles inheritance for nested plugins\\n  - Returns success for valid signatures\\n  - Returns success for core/internal plugins\\n  - Returns success for inherited valid signatures from parent plugins\\n  - Calls `CanLoadPlugin()` for unsigned plugins to check the allowlist\\n  - Returns errors for invalid and modified signatures\\n\\n## Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe allowlist enforcement is implemented in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`. The `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct provides:\\n\\n- `CanLoadPlugin()`: Authorizes plugin loading by:\\n  - Allowing all non-unsigned plugins\\n  - Allowing unsigned plugins in dev mode\\n  - Checking if the plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n  - Denying unsigned plugins not in the allowlist\\n\\n- `ProvideOSSAuthorizer()`: Factory function creating the authorizer from `PluginManagementCfg`\\n\\nThe allowlist configuration is loaded in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` from the `[plugins]` section's `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting, which accepts a comma-separated list of plugin IDs. The list is stored in `pkg/plugins/config/config.go` as `PluginsAllowUnsigned` in `PluginManagementCfg`.\\n\\n## Key Management\\n\\nPublic key retrieval for signature verification is handled through a two-tier system:\\n\\n1. **Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Contains a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key used as fallback\\n2. **Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches keys from the Grafana.com API, updating every 10 days\\n\\nThe key retriever service (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`) acts as a facade, selecting between dynamic and static retrieval based on configuration.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nSignature calculation and validation are integrated into the plugin loading pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` calls `SignatureCalculator.Calculate()` to determine the plugin's signature status before creating the plugin object\\n\\n2. **Validation Stage** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`): `SignatureValidationStep()` creates a validation function that calls `Validation.ValidateSignature()` for each plugin\\n\\n3. **Configuration Integration** (`pkg/plugins/config/config.go`): `PluginManagementCfg` passes the allowlist to the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer`\\n\\n## Models and Interfaces\\n\\nKey types are defined in `pkg/plugins/models.go`:\\n- `SignatureStatus`: \\\"internal\\\", \\\"valid\\\", \\\"invalid\\\", \\\"modified\\\", \\\"unsigned\\\"\\n- `SignatureType`: \\\"grafana\\\", \\\"commercial\\\", \\\"community\\\", \\\"private\\\", \\\"private-glob\\\"\\n\\nCore interfaces in `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`:\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes plugin loading\\n- `SignatureCalculator`: Calculates plugin signature state\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Stores cached public keys\\n\\n## API and Settings\\n\\nThe plugin API (`pkg/api/plugins.go`) and frontend settings (`pkg/api/frontendsettings.go`) expose plugin signature information. Wire dependency injection setup is configured in `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginsintegration.go` and auto-generated in `pkg/server/wire_gen.go`.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
